Wireless remote control for mobile photography The remote control allows mobile photographers to capture photos up to 30 feet from your device. Compatible with ios and android, the remote control can be used with a wide variety of devices
For most devices it is not necessary to download the application, the remote control will automatically pair with your device via bluetooth. For sony xperia s htc an x ​​+ users just download the "360 camera" app from the google play store to use the remote control.
Apply for ios (5.0 above) / android system
(For samsung / moto / google / xiaomi / sony / htc, android 4.1 etc)
Communication: Bluetooth Version.3.0
Transmission frequency: 2.4 ghz-2.4835 ghz
Timer instructions
1. press the power button, led flashing;
2. After calling, press the bluetooth pairing key, led flash slowly. The bluetooth steps to a state that can be searched and combined;
3. use cell phones to match. Led will be out after successful pairing;
4. press the corresponding configuration key. The LED will illuminate after configuration. The product can be used normally at this time.
5. not used for five minutes, the product will automatically enter a latent state. Press the power button to turn off the timer when not in use, to ensure that the battery can be used for a long time.
6. It can be charged with computer devices or mobile power adapter. LED. loading! Took out. Saturation
7 for android phones that cannot be controlled directly through the shutter, download the 360 ​​camera software, open the 360 ​​camera software, click the settings icon in the upper right corner of the phone, advanced settings and then camera settings , set the volume button options for taking pictures.

Black color
Material: ABS
